<h3><span id=".E5.9F.83.E7.B1.B3.C2.B7.E8.AB.BE.E7.89.B9.E9.83.A8.E5.88.86.E6.89.80.E8.91.97.E8.AB.96.E6.96.87.EF.BC.88.E5.BE.B7.E8.AA.9E.EF.BC.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="埃米·諾特部分所著論文（德語）">埃米·諾特部分所著論文（德語）</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%83%E7%B1%B3%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E7%89%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：埃米·諾特部分所著論文（德語）">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><cite class="citation" id="CITEREFNoether1908">Noether, Emmy, <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20130308102907/http://gdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de/no_cache/dms/load/img/?IDDOC=261200" rel="nofollow">Über die Bildung des Formensystems der ternären biquadratischen Form [On Complete Systems of Invariants for Ternary Biquadratic Forms]</a>, Journal für die Reine und Angewandte Mathematik (Germany), 1908, <b>1908</b> (134): 23–90 and two tables <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2020-05-29</span>]</span>, <a class="external text" href="https://dx.doi.org/10.1515%2Fcrll.1908.134.23" rel="nofollow"><span title="數位物件識別號">doi:10.1515/crll.1908.134.23</span></a>, （<a class="external text" href="http://gdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de/no_cache/dms/load/img/?IDDOC=261200" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2013-03-08） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到德语网页">（德语）</span></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9F%83%E7%B1%B3%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E7%89%B9&amp;rft.atitle=%C3%9Cber+die+Bildung+des+Formensystems+der+tern%C3%A4ren+biquadratischen+Form&amp;rft.aufirst=Emmy&amp;rft.aulast=Noether&amp;rft.date=1908&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.issue=134&amp;rft.jtitle=Journal+f%C3%BCr+die+Reine+und+Angewandte+Mathematik&amp;rft.pages=23-90+and+two+tables&amp;rft.volume=1908&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fgdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de%2Fno_cache%2Fdms%2Fload%2Fimg%2F%3FIDDOC%3D261200&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1515%2Fcrll.1908.134.23&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li>
<li><cite class="citation" id="CITEREFNoether1913">———, <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20130308102912/http://gdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de/no_cache/dms/load/img/?IDDOC=244058" rel="nofollow">Rationale Funktionenkörper [Rational Function Fields]</a>, J. Ber. D. DMV (Germany), 1913, <b>22</b>: 316–19 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2020-05-29</span>]</span>, （<a class="external text" href="http://gdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de/no_cache/dms/load/img/?IDDOC=244058" rel="nofollow">原始内容</a>存档于2013-03-08） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到德语网页">（德语）</span></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9F%83%E7%B1%B3%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E7%89%B9&amp;rft.atitle=Rationale+Funktionenk%C3%B6rper&amp;rft.aufirst=Emmy&amp;rft.aulast=Noether&amp;rft.date=1913&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=J.+Ber.+D.+DMV&amp;rft.pages=316-19&amp;rft.volume=22&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fgdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de%2Fno_cache%2Fdms%2Fload%2Fimg%2F%3FIDDOC%3D244058&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li>
<li><cite class="citation" id="CITEREFNoether1915">———, <a class="external text" href="http://www.digizeitschriften.de/download/PPN235181684_0077/log12.pdf" rel="nofollow">Der Endlichkeitssatz der Invarianten endlicher Gruppen [The Finiteness Theorem for Invariants of Finite Groups]</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(PDF)</span>, Mathematische Annalen (Germany), 1915, <b>77</b>: 89–92 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2020-05-29</span>]</span>, <a class="external text" href="https://dx.doi.org/10.1007%2FBF01456821" rel="nofollow"><span title="數位物件識別號">doi:10.1007/BF01456821</span></a>, （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200821202755/http://www.digizeitschriften.de/download/PPN235181684_0077/log12.pdf" rel="nofollow">存档</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(PDF)</span>于2020-08-21） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到德语网页">（德语）</span></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9F%83%E7%B1%B3%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E7%89%B9&amp;rft.atitle=Der+Endlichkeitssatz+der+Invarianten+endlicher+Gruppen&amp;rft.aufirst=Emmy&amp;rft.aulast=Noether&amp;rft.date=1915&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Mathematische+Annalen&amp;rft.pages=89-92&amp;rft.volume=77&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.digizeitschriften.de%2Fdownload%2FPPN235181684_0077%2Flog12.pdf&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1007%2FBF01456821&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li>

<h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.80.A3.E7.B5.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外部連結">外部連結</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%83%E7%B1%B3%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E7%89%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="编辑章节：外部連結">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li><cite class="citation" id="CITEREF約翰·J·奧康納埃德蒙·F·羅伯遜（英语：-{Edmund_F._Robertson}-）">約翰·J·奧康納; <span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Edmund F. Robertson</span></a></span>）</span></span>, <a class="external text" href="http://www-history.mcs.st-andrews.ac.uk/Biographies/Noether_Emmy.html" rel="nofollow">Noether_Emmy</a>, <a href="/wiki/MacTutor%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%8F%B2%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88" title="MacTutor数学史档案">MacTutor数学史档案</a> <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到英语网页">（英语）</span></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9F%83%E7%B1%B3%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E7%89%B9&amp;rft.atitle=Noether_Emmy&amp;rft.au=%3Cspan+class%3D%22ilh-all+%22+data-orig-title%3D%22%E5%9F%83%E5%BE%B7%E8%92%99%C2%B7F%C2%B7%E7%BE%85%E4%BC%AF%E9%81%9C%22+data-lang-code%3D%22en%22+data-lang-name%3D%22%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%22+data-foreign-title%3D%22Edmund+F.+Robertson%22%3E%3Cspan+class%3D%22ilh-page%22%3E%E5%9F%83%E5%BE%B7%E8%92%99%C2%B7F%C2%B7%E7%BE%85%E4%BC%AF%E9%81%9C%3C%2Fspan%3E%3Cspan+class%3D%22noprint+ilh-comment%22%3E%EF%BC%88%3Cspan+class%3D%22ilh-lang%22%3E%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD%3C%2Fspan%3E%3Cspan+class%3D%22ilh-colon%22%3E%EF%BC%9A%3C%2Fspan%3E%3Cspan+class%3D%22ilh-link%22%3E-%7B%3Cspan+lang%3D%22en%22+dir%3D%22auto%22%3EEdmund+F.+Robertson%3C%2Fspan%3E%7D-%3C%2Fspan%3E%EF%BC%89%3C%2Fspan%3E%3C%2Fspan%3E&amp;rft.au=%E7%B4%84%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7J%C2%B7%E5%A5%A7%E5%BA%B7%E7%B4%8D&amp;rft.btitle=-%7Bzh-hans%3AMacTutor%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%8F%B2%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%3Bzh-hant%3AMacTutor%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%8F%B2%E6%AA%94%E6%A1%88%3B%7D-&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww-history.mcs.st-andrews.ac.uk%2FBiographies%2FNoether_Emmy.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li>
<li><cite class="citation"><a class="external text" href="http://www.physikerinnen.de/noetherlebenslauf.html" rel="nofollow">Noether Lebensläufe</a>, Germany: Physikerinnen,  <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2006-10-20</span>]</span>, （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20070929100418/http://www.physikerinnen.de/noetherlebenslauf.html" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2007-09-29） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到德语网页">（德语）</span></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9F%83%E7%B1%B3%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E7%89%B9&amp;rft.btitle=Noether+Lebensl%C3%A4ufe&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.place=Germany&amp;rft.pub=Physikerinnen&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.physikerinnen.de%2Fnoetherlebenslauf.html&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>. 諾特遞交給<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%84%9B%E7%88%BE%E6%9C%97%E6%A0%B9-%E7%B4%90%E5%80%AB%E5%A0%A1%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="愛爾朗根-紐倫堡大學（页面不存在）">埃爾朗根大學</a>的報名信和三份<a href="/wiki/%E5%B1%A5%E6%AD%B7" title="履歷">履歷</a>，其中兩份為手寫，其中第一份為埃米·諾特親筆所寫。</li>
